This is a different resource, scoped to the parent resource, but it may have a different kind.\\n41: \\t// For instance, /pods has the resource \\\"pods\\\" and the kind \\\"Pod\\\", while /pods/foo/status has the resource \\\"pods\\\", the sub resource \\\"status\\\", and the kind \\\"Pod\\\"\\n42: \\t// (because status operates on pods). This is to prevent\\n49: \\t// admission controllers with side effects and a method of reconciliation from being overwhelmed.\\n50: \\t// However, a value of false for this does not mean that the modification will be persisted, because it\\n51: \\t// could still be rejected by a subsequent validation step.\\n52: \\tIsDryRun() bool\\n53: \\t// GetObject is the object from the incoming request prior to default values being applied\\n54: \\tGetObject() runtime.Object\\n55: \\t// GetOldObject is the existing object. \"staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go\", \"symbol\": \"Dispatch\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Kubernetes API server admission controller pipeline is implemented across multiple layers in the staging and production code:\\n\\n## Core Admission Interfaces (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go)\\nThe foundation defines three key interfaces:\\n- `Interface`: Base interface with a Handles() method to check if a controller handles a given operation (CREATE, UPDATE, DELETE, CONNECT)\\n- `MutationInterface`: Extends Interface and defines Admit(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) to mutate admission requests\\n- `ValidationInterface`: Extends Interface and defines Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) to validate requests without mutation\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go)\\nThe `chainAdmissionHandler` type (defined as []Interface) implements the linear chain execution:\\n- `Admit()` method iterates through all handlers, checking if each handles the operation, then calling Admit() on MutationInterface handlers\\n- `Validate()` method similarly processes ValidationInterface handlers\\n- Both methods return immediately on first error\\n- The `NewChainHandler()` function constructs a chain from an array of handlers\\n\\n## Reinvocation Support (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go)\\nThe `reinvoker` wraps the admission chain to support re-invocation policies:\\n- The `Admit()` method first executes the admission chain, then checks the reinvocation context (GetReinvocationContext())\\n- If ShouldReinvoke() returns true, it marks the context as reinvoked and calls Admit() again\\n- This allows plugins that modify the object to trigger re-evaluation of other plugins\\n- The `newReinvocationHandler()` function wraps a chain with reinvocation support\\n\\n## Plugin Registration and Chain Building (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go)\\nThe `Plugins` registry manages admission plugins:\\n- `Register()` registers plugin factories by name during application startup\\n- `NewFromPlugins()` creates an admission.Interface from a list of plugin names by:\\n  1. Loading each plugin using its registered factory\\n  2. Initializing plugins through the PluginInitializer\\n  3. Separating mutating and validating plugins\\n  4. Wrapping the resulting chain with the reinvocationHandler\\n- `InitPlugin()` instantiates a named plugin and validates its initialization\\n\\n## Admission Configuration and Integration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go)\\nThe `AdmissionOptions` struct configures the entire admission pipeline:\\n- `RecommendedPluginOrder` defines the default plugin execution order: NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- The `ApplyTo()` method sets up the admission chain on the server:\\n  1. Reads admission plugin configurations\\n  2. Creates a generic initializer with access to client, informers, and authorization\\n  3. Calls `Plugins.NewFromPlugins()` to build the chain\\n  4. Wraps the chain with metrics via `admissionmetrics.WithStepMetrics()`\\n  5. Assigns the final chain to `Config.AdmissionControl`\\n\\n## Webhook Plugin Registration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go)\\nThe `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` function registers the core admission plugins:\\n- NamespaceLifecycle\\n- ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- ValidatingAdmissionPolicy\\n- MutatingAdmissionPolicy\\n\\n## MutatingAdmissionWebhook Implementation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go)\\nThe mutating webhook plugin:\\n- `Register()` registers the plugin with name \\\"MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- `NewMutatingWebhook()` creates a plugin that:\\n  - Wraps a generic.Webhook with a MutationInterface\\n  - Creates handlers for Connect, Create, Delete, Update operations\\n  - Uses a MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager as the source factory\\n  - Uses a mutating dispatcher to execute webhooks\\n- `Admit()` method delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n## ValidatingAdmissionWebhook Implementation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go)\\nThe validating webhook plugin:\\n- `Register()` registers the plugin with name \\\"ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()` creates a plugin that:\\n  - Wraps a generic.Webhook with a ValidationInterface\\n  - Creates handlers for Connect, Create, Delete, Update operations\\n  - Uses a ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager as the source factory\\n  - Uses a validating dispatcher to execute webhooks\\n- `Validate()` method delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go)\\nThe `Webhook` struct provides the core webhook infrastructure:\\n- Holds references to the hook source (dynamic webhook configurations), client manager, matchers, and dispatcher\\n- `SetExternalKubeInformerFactory()` initializes the hook source from informer factories\\n- `ShouldCallHook()` determines if a webhook matches the request by evaluating:\\n  - Namespace selector\\n  - Object selector\\n  - Rule matching with support for equivalent resources\\n- `Dispatch()` is called by downstream Admit/Validate methods and:\\n  1. Checks if the request is for an exempt admission configuration resource\\n  2. Waits for the webhook to be ready\\n  3. Retrieves webhooks from the hook source\\n  4. Delegates to the dispatcher to execute the webhooks\\n\\n## Webhook Dispatchers\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook execution:\\n\\n### Mutating Dispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go)\\nImplements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface and:\\n- Iterates through mutating webhooks\\n- Evaluates ShouldCallHook() for each webhook\\n- Calls the webhook with the request\\n- Applies patches returned by the webhook to the object\\n- Aggregates audit annotations from webhook responses\\n\\n### Validating Dispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go)\\nImplements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface and:\\n- Iterates through validating webhooks\\n- Evaluates ShouldCallHook() for each webhook\\n- Calls the webhook with the request\\n- Returns immediately on first webhook error (with proper failure policy handling)\\n- Aggregates audit annotations\\n\\n## Webhook Configuration Management\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources from the cluster\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources from the cluster\\n- Both use informers to dynamically track changes to webhook configurations\\n\\n## Admission Policy Plugins\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go`: Implements MutatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based policies)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/plugin.go`: Implements ValidatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based policies)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/generic/plugin.go`: Generic infrastructure for policy plugins\\n\\n## Kube-APIServer Integration\\n- `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go`: across multiple layers in the staging and production code:\\n\\n## Core Admission Interfaces (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go)\\nThe foundation defines three key interfaces:\\n- `Interface`: Base interface with a Handles() method to check if a controller handles a given operation (CREATE, UPDATE, DELETE, CONNECT)\\n- `MutationInterface`: Extends Interface and defines Admit(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) to mutate admission requests\\n- `ValidationInterface`: Extends Interface and defines Validate(ctx, attributes, objectInterfaces) to validate requests without mutation\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go)\\nThe `chainAdmissionHandler` type (defined as []Interface) implements the linear chain execution:\\n- `Admit()` method iterates through all handlers, checking if each handles the operation, then calling Admit() on MutationInterface handlers\\n- `Validate()` method similarly processes ValidationInterface handlers\\n- Both methods return immediately on first error\\n- The `NewChainHandler()` function constructs a chain from an array of handlers\\n\\n## Reinvocation Support (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go)\\nThe `reinvoker` wraps the admission chain to support re-invocation policies:\\n- The `Admit()` method first executes the admission chain, then checks the reinvocation context (GetReinvocationContext())\\n- If ShouldReinvoke() returns true, it marks the context as reinvoked and calls Admit() again\\n- This allows plugins that modify the object to trigger re-evaluation of other plugins\\n- The `newReinvocationHandler()` function wraps a chain with reinvocation support\\n\\n## Plugin Registration and Chain Building (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go)\\nThe `Plugins` registry manages admission plugins:\\n- `Register()` registers plugin factories by name during application startup\\n- `NewFromPlugins()` creates an admission.Interface from a list of plugin names by:\\n  1. Loading each plugin using its registered factory\\n  2. Initializing plugins through the PluginInitializer\\n  3. Separating mutating and validating plugins\\n  4. Wrapping the resulting chain with the reinvocationHandler\\n- `InitPlugin()` instantiates a named plugin and validates its initialization\\n\\n## Admission Configuration and Integration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go)\\nThe `AdmissionOptions` struct configures the entire admission pipeline:\\n- `RecommendedPluginOrder` defines the default plugin execution order: NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- The `ApplyTo()` method sets up the admission chain on the server:\\n  1. Reads admission plugin configurations\\n  2. Creates a generic initializer with access to client, informers, and authorization\\n  3. Calls `Plugins.NewFromPlugins()` to build the chain\\n  4. Wraps the chain with metrics via `admissionmetrics.WithStepMetrics()`\\n  5. Assigns the final chain to `Config.AdmissionControl`\\n\\n## Webhook Plugin Registration (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go)\\nThe `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` function registers the core admission plugins:\\n- NamespaceLifecycle\\n- ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\n- ValidatingAdmissionPolicy\\n- MutatingAdmissionPolicy\\n\\n## MutatingAdmissionWebhook Implementation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go)\\nThe mutating webhook plugin:\\n- `Register()` registers the plugin with name \\\"MutatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- `NewMutatingWebhook()` creates a plugin that:\\n  - Wraps a generic.Webhook with a MutationInterface\\n  - Creates handlers for Connect, Create, Delete, Update operations\\n  - Uses a MutatingWebhookConfigurationManager as the source factory\\n  - Uses a mutating dispatcher to execute webhooks\\n- `Admit()` method delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n## ValidatingAdmissionWebhook Implementation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go)\\nThe validating webhook plugin:\\n- `Register()` registers the plugin with name \\\"ValidatingAdmissionWebhook\\\"\\n- `NewValidatingAdmissionWebhook()` creates a plugin that:\\n  - Wraps a generic.Webhook with a ValidationInterface\\n  - Creates handlers for Connect, Create, Delete, Update operations\\n  - Uses a ValidatingWebhookConfigurationManager as the source factory\\n  - Uses a validating dispatcher to execute webhooks\\n- `Validate()` method delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n\\n## Generic Webhook Execution (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go)\\nThe `Webhook` struct provides the core webhook infrastructure:\\n- Holds references to the hook source (dynamic webhook configurations), client manager, matchers, and dispatcher\\n- `SetExternalKubeInformerFactory()` initializes the hook source from informer factories\\n- `ShouldCallHook()` determines if a webhook matches the request by evaluating:\\n  - Namespace selector\\n  - Object selector\\n  - Rule matching with support for equivalent resources\\n- `Dispatch()` is called by downstream Admit/Validate methods and:\\n  1. Checks if the request is for an exempt admission configuration resource\\n  2. Waits for the webhook to be ready\\n  3. Retrieves webhooks from the hook source\\n  4. Delegates to the dispatcher to execute the webhooks\\n\\n## Webhook Dispatchers\\nTwo dispatcher implementations handle webhook execution:\\n\\n### Mutating Dispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go)\\nImplements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface and:\\n- Iterates through mutating webhooks\\n- Evaluates ShouldCallHook() for each webhook\\n- Calls the webhook with the request\\n- Applies patches returned by the webhook to the object\\n- Aggregates audit annotations from webhook responses\\n\\n### Validating Dispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go)\\nImplements the `generic.Dispatcher` interface and:\\n- Iterates through validating webhooks\\n- Evaluates ShouldCallHook() for each webhook\\n- Calls the webhook with the request\\n- Returns immediately on first webhook error (with proper failure policy handling)\\n- Aggregates audit annotations\\n\\n## Webhook Configuration Management\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources from the cluster\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources from the cluster\\n- Both use informers to dynamically track changes to webhook configurations\\n\\n## Admission Policy Plugins\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go`: Implements MutatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based policies)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/plugin.go`: Implements ValidatingAdmissionPolicy (CEL-based policies)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/generic/plugin.go`: Generic infrastructure for policy plugins\\n\\n## Kube-APIServer Integration\\n- `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go`:
